You can reach our Ambassador for further information: Jodi Voice: world_at_large82@yahoo.com Emilia Gaston: emiliagastonphoto@gmail.com Snowy Voice: snowy.voice@uitct.com . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . Sunday, January 20, 2019 at 1:30 PM – 4 PM Our AIHD Matrilineal Leaders will lead the Dallas Women's March . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . Start Location: St. Paul UMC Dallas Hosted by American Indian Heritage Day in Texas . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . MMIW Texas and American Indian Heritage Day in Texas proudly invite all members of the DFW American Indian community and our allies to join us as we LEAD the Dallas Women's March! MMIW Texas was created to raise awareness, share information and resources, and offer support to families revolving around the epidemic of Missing and Murdered Indigenous Women (MMIW). The Dallas Women's March has kindly provided the American Indian community the opportunity to lead this year's march and with this platform, we will be advocating for awareness of MMIW and issues affecting indigenous women and communities. Our participation will include the following elements at the beginning of the march: • Land acknowledgement • Prayer • Song(s) We ask that those who join us: • Wear red or dress out in your traditional regalia! • Make a sign to bring to the march! • Bring a friend Come ready to be front and center! We will be carrying the Dallas Women's March banner and leading the march to the end point at City Hall, so let's #REPRESENT our amazing indigenous communities and nations! Start Location: St. Paul UMC Dallas Hosted by American Indian Heritage Day in Texas . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . MMIW Texas and American Indian Heritage Day in Texas proudly invite all members of the DFW American Indian community and our allies to join us as we LEAD the Dallas Women's March! MMIW Texas was created to raise awareness, share information and resources, and offer support to families revolving around the epidemic of Missing and Murdered Indigenous Women (MMIW). The Dallas Women's March has kindly provided the American Indian community the opportunity to lead this year's march and with this platform, we will be advocating for awareness of MMIW and issues affecting indigenous women and communities. Our participation will include the following elements at the beginning of the march: • Land acknowledgement • Prayer • Song(s) We ask that those who join us: • Wear red or dress out in your traditional regalia! • Make a sign to bring to the march! • Bring a friend Come ready to be front and center! We will be carrying the Dallas Women's March banner and leading the march to the end point at City Hall, so let's #REPRESENT our amazing indigenous communities and nations! MMIW Texas and American Indian Heritage Day in Texas proudly invite all members of the DFW American Indian community and our allies to join us as we LEAD the Dallas Women's March! MMIW Texas was created to raise awareness, share information and resources, and offer support to families revolving around the epidemic of Missing and Murdered Indigenous Women (MMIW). The Dallas Women's March has kindly provided the American Indian community the opportunity to lead this year's march and with this platform, we will be advocating for awareness of MMIW and issues affecting indigenous women and communities. Our participation will include the following elements at the beginning of the march: • Land acknowledgement • Prayer • Song(s) We ask that those who join us: • Wear red or dress out in your traditional regalia! • Make a sign to bring to the march! • Bring a friend Come ready to be front and center! We will be carrying the Dallas Women's March banner and leading the march to the end point at City Hall, so let's #REPRESENT our amazing indigenous communities and nations! येथे फोडतो - हाय काय अन् नाय काय ! सूर्य केंद्राच्या डोक्यावर सूर्यापासून नेहमी मोजल्यास उजव्या बाजूला पहिले … १. संत ज्ञानेश्वर … आता याच क्रमाने तुम्हीं पुढील नांवें सांगा बरं. या सप्ताहांत दररोज 18:50:39","updated":"2022-01-06 20:10:35","type":"photo","description":"#HCMAE_BIRTHDAY\n\n•• Today is 52nd Birthday of Eminent Hindustani Classical Vocalist of Mewati Gharana Pandit Suman Ghosh (6 January 1967) ••\n\nPandit Suman Ghosh (born 6 January 1967) is an internationally acclaimed Hindustani Classical Vocalist of the Mewati Gharana of Hindustani Classical Music and a torch-bearing disciple of Sangeet Martand Pandit Jasraj. He is the founder and President of the Center for Indian Classical Music of Houston (CICMH).\n\n• Early life :\nPandit Suman Ghosh was born on January 6, 1967 to Smt. Monica Ghosh and Shri Biman Krishna Ghosh. Pandit Ghosh started his musical education under the guidance of his mother and unequivocal support of his father. Pandit Suman Ghosh continued his formal training, first under Maestro Pandit Shrikant Bakre, a torch-bearer of the great Ustad Amir Khan. Then, he was groomed by Padma Bhushan Pandit Jnan Prakash Ghosh for several years. Finally, Pandit Suman Ghosh underwent several years of intense training on and off stage, with the living legend, Padma Vibhushan Sangeet Martand Pandit Jasraj.\n\nBesides pursuing music, he has earned a Bachelor's and a master's degree from University of Calcutta.\n\n• Career :\nPandit Suman Ghosh, is a performer of note and is also committed to the cause of spreading Hindustani Classical Music and its rich and age-old tradition not only in India, but throughout the world. His vision is to enrich every individual by musically awakening their inner spiritual self. He has dedicated the past 30 years of his life to selflessly serving the global human community through his performances and spreading this tradition through his teachings, thus promoting and cultivating this beautiful art in particular and Indian Culture as a whole.\n\n• The Performer :\nPandit Suman Ghosh gave his first full concert at the age of 12. He soon became one of the youngest ever artists in All India Radio to perform in three different genres.\n\nAs an established musician, he performs regularly all over the United States, Canada, Europe and India. In India, he has performed in several prestigious events like Pandit Motiram Pandit Maniram Sangeet Samaroh, Saptak Annual Festival of Music and the Malhar Festival. He has also had the privilege of singing before Dr. A P J Abdul Kalam, former President of India, both at Rashtrapati Bhavan in 2000 and during Dr. Kalam's visit to USA in 2011.\nRead more about him here » https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Suman_Ghosh\n\nOn his Birthday, Hindustani Classical Music And Everything wishes him a long, healthy and active musical life ahead. :)","message":"Wishing our beloved Pujya Guruji, Pandit @Suman Ghosh Ji, a very HAPPY BIRTHDAY !
